module EN_Flags_Craft
{
	imports
	{
		Base
	}

	recipe Craft Blank Flag
	{
		keep Scissors,
		keep Needle/SewingKit,
		Thread=2,
		Sheet=6,

		Result:BlankFlag,
		Time:1200.0,
		Prop1:Needle,
		Prop2:Sheet,
		AnimNode:RipSheets,
		Category:Flags,
	}
	

	/* Nations - Current */

	recipe Paint Flag of Afghanistan
	{
		keep PaintGreen,
		keep PaintWhite,
		keep PaintBlack,
		keep PaintYellow,
		keep Paintbrush,
		BlankFlag,

		Result:ENFAfghanistan,
		Time:150.0,
		Prop1:Paintbrush,
		Prop2:Sheet,
		AnimNode:SawLog,
		Category:Flags,
	}
